
# CADAgent

CADAgent is an AI-powered system that generates and manipulates parametric 3D models using **OpenSCAD** and **DeepAgent**. It leverages **GPT-4.1** for interpreting user instructions and generating structured OpenSCAD code, enabling both text and image-based inputs to produce 3D geometries.

---

## Features

- Generate OpenSCAD models from **natural language instructions**.
- Support for **image-guided CAD generation** (input images like wheels or components).
- Modular and parametric design approach for **reusable components**.
- Sandbox execution using **LocalShellBackend** for safe OpenSCAD compilation.
- Persistent memory and session handling via **DeepAgent MemorySaver**.

---

## Installation

1. Clone the repository:

```bash
git clone https://github.com/Alton1998/CADAgent.git
cd CADAgent
````

2. Create a virtual environment and activate it:

```bash
python -m venv venv
# On Windows
venv\Scripts\activate
# On macOS/Linux
source venv/bin/activate
```

3. Install dependencies:

```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

4. Install OpenSCAD:

* **Windows:** Download from [OpenSCAD](https://www.openscad.org/downloads.html)
* **macOS:** `brew install openscad`
* **Linux:** `sudo apt install openscad`

5. Add OpenSCAD to your system `PATH` (if not automatically added).

6. Create a `.env` file with your API keys:

```env
OPENAI_API_KEY=your_openai_api_key_here
MODEL=openai:gpt-4.1-2025-04-14
```

---

## Usage

Run the agent:

```bash
python agent.py
```

1. Enter a natural language description for the 3D object.
2. Optionally, provide an **image URL** to guide the CAD generation.
3. The agent will generate OpenSCAD code and execute it in the sandbox.
4. Generated STL/SCAD files are stored in the `sandbox/` folder.

Example:

```
Enter your message: I want to create a simple parametric wheel
Enter image url: https://raw.githubusercontent.com/.../wheel.png
```

---

## Project Structure

```
CADAgent/
â”œâ”€â”€ main.py                  # Entry point for the agent
â”œâ”€â”€ subagent/                # Subagents for specialized tasks
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ openscad_subagent.py
â”œâ”€â”€ prompts/                 # System prompts for GPT-4.1
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ COORDINATOR_SYSTEM_PROMPT.py
â”œâ”€â”€ utils/                   # Helper functions (formatting, utilities)
â”œâ”€â”€ sandbox/                 # Temporary outputs (STL/SCAD)
â”œâ”€â”€ memory/                  # Persistent agent memory
â”œâ”€â”€ requirements.txt
â””â”€â”€ .env                     # API keys and environment variables (ignored by git)
```

---

## Notes

* Always use **raw image URLs** (e.g., `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/...`) for image inputs.
* `.env` and sandbox outputs are ignored in Git (`.gitignore`) for security and cleanliness.
* The system is designed to **separate generation from compilation**, so OpenSCAD code is always first generated by GPT-4.1 and then executed safely.

â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ Here is a clean, commented OpenSCAD code for a simple car model as you      â”‚
â”‚ requested:                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Simple parametric car model                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Car body parameters                                                      â”‚
â”‚ body_length = 60;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ body_width = 30;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ body_height = 15;                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel parameters                                                         â”‚
â”‚ wheel_radius = 7;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ wheel_width = 5;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_radius = 2;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_length = body_width + 2 * (wheel_width + 1);                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel positions                                                          â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_x = body_length / 2 - wheel_radius - 3;                        â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_y = body_width / 2 + wheel_width / 2 + 1;                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Main car module                                                          â”‚
â”‚ module simple_car() {                                                       â”‚
â”‚     // Body                                                                 â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         union() {                                                           â”‚
â”‚             // Main body                                                    â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,wheel_radius + 1])                               â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚             // Cabin (simple block for windshield)                          â”‚
â”‚             translate([6,0,wheel_radius + body_height + 1])                 â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚         }                                                                   â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚     // Wheels and axles                                                     â”‚
â”‚     for(side=[-1,1]) {  // Front/Rear wheels                                â”‚
â”‚         // Axles                                                            â”‚
â”‚         translate()                                                         â”‚
â”‚             rotate([90,0,0])                                                â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=axle_length, r=axle_radius, center=true);        â”‚
â”‚         // Left and Right wheels at each axle                               â”‚
â”‚         for(lr=[-1,1])                                                      â”‚
â”‚             translate()                                                     â”‚
â”‚                 rotate([0,90,0])                                            â”‚
â”‚                     wheel();                                                â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel module (with simple hubcap)                                        â”‚
â”‚ module wheel() {                                                            â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         color("black")                                                      â”‚
â”‚             cylinder(h=wheel_width, r=wheel_radius, center=true);           â”‚
â”‚         color("silver")                                                     â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,0])                                              â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=wheel_width+0.2, r=wheel_radius*0.6,             â”‚
â”‚ center=true);                                                               â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Render the car                                                           â”‚

â”‚    ID: call_R2MzmqrB5hVUNot6DeTJvyls                                        â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ ğŸ”§ Tool Output â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Here is the OpenSCAD code for a simple parametric car model, including a    â”‚
â”‚ rectangular body, four wheels, and axles. The code is modular and           â”‚
â”‚ well-commented for clarity.                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ Here is a clean, commented OpenSCAD code for a simple car model as you      â”‚
â”‚ requested:                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Simple parametric car model                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Car body parameters                                                      â”‚
â”‚ body_length = 60;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ body_width = 30;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ body_height = 15;                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel parameters                                                         â”‚
â”‚ wheel_radius = 7;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ wheel_width = 5;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_radius = 2;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_length = body_width + 2 * (wheel_width + 1);                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel positions                                                          â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_x = body_length / 2 - wheel_radius - 3;                        â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_y = body_width / 2 + wheel_width / 2 + 1;                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Main car module                                                          â”‚
â”‚ module simple_car() {                                                       â”‚
â”‚     // Body                                                                 â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         union() {                                                           â”‚
â”‚             // Main body                                                    â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,wheel_radius + 1])                               â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚             // Cabin (simple block for windshield)                          â”‚
â”‚             translate([6,0,wheel_radius + body_height + 1])                 â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚         }                                                                   â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚     // Wheels and axles                                                     â”‚
â”‚     for(side=[-1,1]) {  // Front/Rear wheels                                â”‚
â”‚         // Axles                                                            â”‚
â”‚         translate()                                                         â”‚
â”‚             rotate([90,0,0])                                                â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=axle_length, r=axle_radius, center=true);        â”‚
â”‚         // Left and Right wheels at each axle                               â”‚
â”‚         for(lr=[-1,1])                                                      â”‚
â”‚             translate()                                                     â”‚
â”‚                 rotate([0,90,0])                                            â”‚
â”‚                     wheel();                                                â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel module (with simple hubcap)                                        â”‚
â”‚ module wheel() {                                                            â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         color("black")                                                      â”‚
â”‚             cylinder(h=wheel_width, r=wheel_radius, center=true);           â”‚
â”‚         color("silver")                                                     â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,0])                                              â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=wheel_width+0.2, r=wheel_radius*0.6,             â”‚
â”‚ center=true);                                                               â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Render the car                                                           â”‚
â”‚ simple_car();                                                               â”‚

â”‚    ID: call_R2MzmqrB5hVUNot6DeTJvyls                                        â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ ğŸ”§ Tool Output â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Here is the OpenSCAD code for a simple parametric car model, including a    â”‚
â”‚ rectangular body, four wheels, and axles. The code is modular and           â”‚
â”‚ well-commented for clarity.                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ Here is a clean, commented OpenSCAD code for a simple car model as you      â”‚
â”‚ requested:                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Simple parametric car model                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Car body parameters                                                      â”‚
â”‚ body_length = 60;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ body_width = 30;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ body_height = 15;                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel parameters                                                         â”‚
â”‚ wheel_radius = 7;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ wheel_width = 5;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_radius = 2;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_length = body_width + 2 * (wheel_width + 1);                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel positions                                                          â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_x = body_length / 2 - wheel_radius - 3;                        â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_y = body_width / 2 + wheel_width / 2 + 1;                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Main car module                                                          â”‚
â”‚ module simple_car() {                                                       â”‚
â”‚     // Body                                                                 â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         union() {                                                           â”‚
â”‚             // Main body                                                    â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,wheel_radius + 1])                               â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚             // Cabin (simple block for windshield)                          â”‚
â”‚             translate([6,0,wheel_radius + body_height + 1])                 â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚         }                                                                   â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚     // Wheels and axles                                                     â”‚
â”‚     for(side=[-1,1]) {  // Front/Rear wheels                                â”‚
â”‚         // Axles                                                            â”‚
â”‚         translate()                                                         â”‚
â”‚             rotate([90,0,0])                                                â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=axle_length, r=axle_radius, center=true);        â”‚
â”‚         // Left and Right wheels at each axle                               â”‚
â”‚         for(lr=[-1,1])                                                      â”‚
â”‚             translate()                                                     â”‚
â”‚                 rotate([0,90,0])                                            â”‚
â”‚                     wheel();                                                â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel module (with simple hubcap)                                        â”‚
â”‚ module wheel() {                                                            â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         color("black")                                                      â”‚
â”‚             cylinder(h=wheel_width, r=wheel_radius, center=true);           â”‚
â”‚         color("silver")                                                     â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,0])                                              â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=wheel_width+0.2, r=wheel_radius*0.6,             â”‚
â”‚ center=true);                                                               â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Render the car                                                           â”‚
â”‚ simple_car();                                                               â”‚

â”‚   "content": "// Simple parametric car model\n\n// Car body                 â”‚
â”‚ parameters\nbody_length = 60;\nbody_width = 30;\nbody_height = 15;\n\n//    â”‚
â”‚ Wheel parameters\nwheel_radius = 7;\nwheel_width = 5;\naxle_radius =        â”‚
â”‚ 2;\naxle_length = body_width + 2 * (wheel_width + 1);\n\n// Wheel           â”‚
â”‚ positions\nwheel_offset_x = body_length / 2 - wheel_radius -                â”‚
â”‚ 3;\nwheel_offset_y = body_width / 2 + wheel_width / 2 + 1;\n\n// Main car   â”‚

â”‚ union() {\n            // Main body\n                                       â”‚
â”‚ translate([0,0,wheel_radius + 1])\n                cube(, center=true);\n   â”‚

â”‚ translate([6,0,wheel_radius + body_height + 1])\n                cube(,     â”‚
â”‚ center=true);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Wheels and axles\n                â”‚
â”‚ for(side=[-1,1]) {  // Front/Rear wheels\n        // Axles\n                â”‚

â”‚    ID: call_R2MzmqrB5hVUNot6DeTJvyls                                        â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ ğŸ”§ Tool Output â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Here is the OpenSCAD code for a simple parametric car model, including a    â”‚
â”‚ rectangular body, four wheels, and axles. The code is modular and           â”‚
â”‚ well-commented for clarity.                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ Here is a clean, commented OpenSCAD code for a simple car model as you      â”‚
â”‚ requested:                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Simple parametric car model                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Car body parameters                                                      â”‚
â”‚ body_length = 60;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ body_width = 30;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ body_height = 15;                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel parameters                                                         â”‚
â”‚ wheel_radius = 7;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ wheel_width = 5;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_radius = 2;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_length = body_width + 2 * (wheel_width + 1);                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel positions                                                          â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_x = body_length / 2 - wheel_radius - 3;                        â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_y = body_width / 2 + wheel_width / 2 + 1;                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Main car module                                                          â”‚
â”‚ module simple_car() {                                                       â”‚
â”‚     // Body                                                                 â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         union() {                                                           â”‚
â”‚             // Main body                                                    â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,wheel_radius + 1])                               â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚             // Cabin (simple block for windshield)                          â”‚
â”‚             translate([6,0,wheel_radius + body_height + 1])                 â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚         }                                                                   â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚     // Wheels and axles                                                     â”‚
â”‚     for(side=[-1,1]) {  // Front/Rear wheels                                â”‚
â”‚         // Axles                                                            â”‚
â”‚         translate()                                                         â”‚
â”‚             rotate([90,0,0])                                                â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=axle_length, r=axle_radius, center=true);        â”‚
â”‚         // Left and Right wheels at each axle                               â”‚
â”‚         for(lr=[-1,1])                                                      â”‚
â”‚             translate()                                                     â”‚
â”‚                 rotate([0,90,0])                                            â”‚
â”‚                     wheel();                                                â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel module (with simple hubcap)                                        â”‚
â”‚ module wheel() {                                                            â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         color("black")                                                      â”‚
â”‚             cylinder(h=wheel_width, r=wheel_radius, center=true);           â”‚
â”‚         color("silver")                                                     â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,0])                                              â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=wheel_width+0.2, r=wheel_radius*0.6,             â”‚
â”‚ center=true);                                                               â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Render the car                                                           â”‚
â”‚ simple_car();                                                               â”‚

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ ğŸ”§ Tool Output â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Here is the OpenSCAD code for a simple parametric car model, including a    â”‚
â”‚ rectangular body, four wheels, and axles. The code is modular and           â”‚
â”‚ well-commented for clarity.                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ Here is a clean, commented OpenSCAD code for a simple car model as you      â”‚
â”‚ requested:                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Simple parametric car model                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Car body parameters                                                      â”‚
â”‚ body_length = 60;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ body_width = 30;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ body_height = 15;                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel parameters                                                         â”‚
â”‚ wheel_radius = 7;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ wheel_width = 5;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_radius = 2;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_length = body_width + 2 * (wheel_width + 1);                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel positions                                                          â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_x = body_length / 2 - wheel_radius - 3;                        â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_y = body_width / 2 + wheel_width / 2 + 1;                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Main car module                                                          â”‚
â”‚ module simple_car() {                                                       â”‚
â”‚     // Body                                                                 â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         union() {                                                           â”‚
â”‚             // Main body                                                    â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,wheel_radius + 1])                               â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚             // Cabin (simple block for windshield)                          â”‚
â”‚             translate([6,0,wheel_radius + body_height + 1])                 â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚         }                                                                   â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚     // Wheels and axles                                                     â”‚
â”‚     for(side=[-1,1]) {  // Front/Rear wheels                                â”‚
â”‚         // Axles                                                            â”‚
â”‚         translate()                                                         â”‚
â”‚             rotate([90,0,0])                                                â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=axle_length, r=axle_radius, center=true);        â”‚
â”‚         // Left and Right wheels at each axle                               â”‚
â”‚         for(lr=[-1,1])                                                      â”‚
â”‚             translate()                                                     â”‚
â”‚                 rotate([0,90,0])                                            â”‚
â”‚                     wheel();                                                â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel module (with simple hubcap)                                        â”‚
â”‚ module wheel() {                                                            â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         color("black")                                                      â”‚
â”‚             cylinder(h=wheel_width, r=wheel_radius, center=true);           â”‚
â”‚         color("silver")                                                     â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,0])                                              â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=wheel_width+0.2, r=wheel_radius*0.6,             â”‚
â”‚ center=true);                                                               â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Render the car                                                           â”‚
â”‚ simple_car();                                                               â”‚

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ ğŸ”§ Tool Output â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Here is the OpenSCAD code for a simple parametric car model, including a    â”‚
â”‚ rectangular body, four wheels, and axles. The code is modular and           â”‚
â”‚ well-commented for clarity.                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ Here is a clean, commented OpenSCAD code for a simple car model as you      â”‚
â”‚ requested:                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Simple parametric car model                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Car body parameters                                                      â”‚
â”‚ body_length = 60;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ body_width = 30;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ body_height = 15;                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel parameters                                                         â”‚
â”‚ wheel_radius = 7;                                                           â”‚
â”‚ wheel_width = 5;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_radius = 2;                                                            â”‚
â”‚ axle_length = body_width + 2 * (wheel_width + 1);                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel positions                                                          â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_x = body_length / 2 - wheel_radius - 3;                        â”‚
â”‚ wheel_offset_y = body_width / 2 + wheel_width / 2 + 1;                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Main car module                                                          â”‚
â”‚ module simple_car() {                                                       â”‚
â”‚     // Body                                                                 â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         union() {                                                           â”‚
â”‚             // Main body                                                    â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,wheel_radius + 1])                               â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚             // Cabin (simple block for windshield)                          â”‚
â”‚             translate([6,0,wheel_radius + body_height + 1])                 â”‚
â”‚                 cube(, center=true);                                        â”‚
â”‚         }                                                                   â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚     // Wheels and axles                                                     â”‚
â”‚     for(side=[-1,1]) {  // Front/Rear wheels                                â”‚
â”‚         // Axles                                                            â”‚
â”‚         translate()                                                         â”‚
â”‚             rotate([90,0,0])                                                â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=axle_length, r=axle_radius, center=true);        â”‚
â”‚         // Left and Right wheels at each axle                               â”‚
â”‚         for(lr=[-1,1])                                                      â”‚
â”‚             translate()                                                     â”‚
â”‚                 rotate([0,90,0])                                            â”‚
â”‚                     wheel();                                                â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Wheel module (with simple hubcap)                                        â”‚
â”‚ module wheel() {                                                            â”‚
â”‚     difference() {                                                          â”‚
â”‚         color("black")                                                      â”‚
â”‚             cylinder(h=wheel_width, r=wheel_radius, center=true);           â”‚
â”‚         color("silver")                                                     â”‚
â”‚             translate([0,0,0])                                              â”‚
â”‚                 cylinder(h=wheel_width+0.2, r=wheel_radius*0.6,             â”‚
â”‚ center=true);                                                               â”‚
â”‚     }                                                                       â”‚
â”‚ }                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚ // Render the car                                                           â”‚
â”‚ simple_car();                                                               â”‚
